 duusari ore peedita lagaataar is koshish main lagi rahi ki police maamle kii jaanch ko gambhirtha se le
 Raid on the pretext of 'ram Katha'! For the last two days, CID police investigated all the properties of the monastery in Uttara Kannada district
 iske saath hi police ne math main rahane vaale staff se bhi kadi poochtacha kii

 The Supreme Court on Thursday told the lower court of Gujarat that during the 2002 riots in Ahmedabad, the final orders on the closure report of the Special Investigation Team in the Gulberg Housing Society case should not be pronounced
 nyaayamurti dike jain, nyaayamurti pi sadashivam or nyaayamurti aftab alam kii khandpeeth ne congress ke purv saansad ehsaan jaafaree kii vidhwaa jakia jaafaree kii yachika par sunwaayee ke dauraan kaha, ‘‘maamla band karne kii report par antim aadesh nahin sunaaya jayega
 The judges have also sought a response from the Gujarat government in the matter
 ahmedabad kii adaalat ne gat varsh 27 november ko vishesh jaanch dal kii maamla band karne sambandhi report sweekaar kar lee thi
 The report was filed by the investigation team on 13 March 2012
 godhra cond ke baad gujarat main hue dangon ke nau maamalon main nyaayalay kii madad ke liye niyukt varisht adhivaktaa harish salve ne sambandhit ek ghatnakram main kaha ki vah mukhya gavaahon ko ‘anyatra’ rakhane or unhen lagaataar suraksha pradaan karne ke liye ek arji daakhil kar rahe hai
 Meanwhile, the judges have expressed surprise at the Justice GT Nanavati Commission constituted to investigate these riots, summoning members of the Special Investigation Team and seeking its report despite the apex court's clear order
 nyaayadhishon ne kaha ki nyaayalay pehle hi spasht kar chukaa he ki jaanch dal kii report sirf uske hi saamne pesh kii jaaegi
 This commission was formed by the state government
 nyaayadhishon ne kaha, ‘‘hamaara pehle kaa aadesh aspasht nahin he
 In fact, we told the Special Investigation Team that it would not give any information
 
 The court gave the order on September 12, 2011 in the case related to providing documents to Zakia Jafri
 nyaayalay ne kendriya jaanch beuro ke purv nideshak aarake raghavan kii adhyakshata vaale vishesh jaanch dal ko apni antim report sthaneey adaalat ko bhejne kaa nirdesh diya tha
 The investigation team had investigated several cases of Gujarat riots including Gulberg Housing Society
 vishesh jaanch dal ke sadsy varisht police adhikari eke malhotra se vishesh rup se gulburg houseing sosayadi cond kii jaanch karne kaa aagrah kiya gaya tha
 He filed his report in a sealed envelope in the apex court
 jakia jaafaree ne eke malhotra dwaara daakhil report sahit is maamle kii jaanch se sambandhit dastavej muhaiyaa karaane se nichali adaalat ke inkaar karne par sheersh adaalat main vishesh anumati yachika daayar kar rakhi he
 She wants these documents to file a protest petition on the report of the Special Investigation Team to close the case
 unka tark he ki jaanch se sambandhit dastavej nahin milane ke kaaran vah jaanch dal kii report par virodh yachika daayar nahin kar paa rahi hai
 On February 28, 2002, at the Gulbarg Housing Society in Ahmedabad, 69 people including ex-mp Ehsan Jaffrey were killed by an angry mob
 ahmedabad kii adaalat ne 16 july, 2012 ko jakia jaafaree ko ye dastavej muhaiyaa karaane se inkaar kar diya tha
 Zakia's lawyer Kamini Jaiswal said that the November 27 order and order not to provide documents about the closure of the case was becoming a hindrance to the victim's right to file a protest petition
 nichali adaalat ne kaha tha ki jakia jaafaree samay biit jane ke kaaran vishesh jaanch dal kii report ke khilaaf virodh yachika daayar karne kaa adhikaar ganvaa chuki he
 The court said that despite giving sufficient time, they have not filed a protest petition
 is report main gujarat ke mukhyamantri narendra modi ko clin chit di gayi thi
 The comments adaalat ne kaha tha ki jakia jaafaree vishesh jaanch dal kii report ke khilaaf maukhik rup se apana virodh darj kara sakati hai
 In March 2012, the Special Investigation Team submitted its final report in the Gulberg Society case to the apex court
 vishesh jaanch dal ne report kii ek prati jakia jaafaree ko bhi di thi taaki vah do maheene ke nirdhaarit samay ke bheetar virodh yachika daayar kar saken lekin unhone aisa nahin kiya tha
 a division bench of Justice DK Jain, Justice p Sadasivam and Justice Aftab Alam said during the hearing on the petition of Zakia Jafri, widow of former Congress MP Ehsan Jafri, "the final order will not be heard on the closure report
" ’’ nyaayadhishon ne iske saath hi is maamle main gujarat sarkaar se jawaab maanga he
 On November 27 last year, the Ahmedabad court accepted the report of the Special Investigation Team to close the case
 jaanch dal ne yah report 13 march 2012 ko daayar kii thi
 Senior advocate Harish Salve, who was appointed to assist the court in nine cases of riots in Gujarat after the Godhra carnage, said in a related development that he was filing an application to keep the key witnesses 'elsewhere' and provide them continued protection
 Huh
 is bich, nyaayadhishon ne in dangon kii jaanch ke liye gathit nyaayamurti jiti nanavati ayog dwaara vishesh jaanch dal ke sadasyon ko talab karne or sheersh adaalat ke spasht aadesh ke baavjood uski report maangane par achraj vyakt kiya he
 The judges said that the court has already clarified that the report of the investigation team will be presented only before it
 is ayog kaa gathan rajya sarkaar ne kiya tha
 The judges said, "our earlier order is unclear
 vastav main hamane vishesh jaanch dal se kaha tha ki vah koi jaankaree nahin degaa
 
 ’’ nyaayalay ne jakia jaafaree ko dastavej muhaiyaa karaane se sambandhit maamle main 12 sitambar, 2011 ko yah aadesh diya tha
 The court directed the Special Investigation Team headed by former Central Bureau of Investigation director RK Raghavan to send its final report to the local court
 jaanch dal ne hi gulburg houseing sosayadi sahit gujarat dangon ke kai maamalon kii jaanch kii thi
 Senior police officer AK Malhotra, a member of the special investigation team, was specifically urged to investigate the Gulberg Housing Society scandal
 unhone apni report silband lipaphe main sheersh adaalat main daayar kii thi
 Zakia Jafri has filed a special leave petition in the apex court on the refusal of the lower court to provide documents related to the investigation of the case, including the report filed by AK Malhotra
 vah vishesh jaanch dal kii maamla band karne sambandhi report par virodh yachika daayar karne ke liye ye dastavej chaahati hai
 She argues that due to lack of documents related to the investigation, she is not able to file a protest petition on the investigation team's report
 ahmedabad sthit gulburg houseing sosayadi main 28 farvari, 2002 ko hue kand main ugr bheed ne purv saansad ehsaan jaafaree sahit 69 vyaktiyon kii hatya kar di thi
 On 16 July 2012, an Ahmedabad court refused to provide these documents to Zakia Jafri
 jakia kii vakil kamini jaiswal kaa kahana tha ki yah maamla band karne ke bare main 27 november ke aadesh or dastavej muhaiyaa nahin karana peedit ke virodh yachika daayar karne ke adhikaar main baadhak ban rahaa he
 The lower court had said that Zakia Jafri lost the right to file a protest petition against the report of the Special Investigation Team due to the passage of time
 adaalat kaa kahana tha ki paryaapt samay dene ke baavjood unhone virodh yachika daayar nahin kii he
 In this report, a clean chit was given to Gujarat Chief Minister Narendra Modi
 tippaniyan The court had said that Zakia Jafri can verbally register her protest against the Special Investigation Team report
 vishesh jaanch dal ne march 2012 main gulburg sosayadi prakaran main apni antim report sheersh adaalat ko saunpi thi
